3-0 Decks from Grand Prix Lyon's First Booster Draft
====================================================



 Posted in [GRAND PRIX LYON 2015](/en/events/coverage/gplyo15)
 on November 1, 2015 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/person/henke_author.jpg)
By Tobi Henke












 Want to know what it takes to go 3-0 in *Battle for Zendikar* Booster Draft? Of course you do. Well, it takes a deck like one of these. Below you can find the lists of all the 3-0 decks from the first draft of the day. It may be interesting to note that white-black was the most represented color combination (with eight copies) followed by blue-black (four), white-blue, and green-white (three each). However, while this shows a clear trend, all ten two-color pairs have at least one entry here!



(Note that no one went 3-0 in Draft Pod 8.)










#### Michael Hitz, 3-0 Grand Prix Lyon Booster Draft #1, Pod #1


##### 




![](https://web.archive.org/web/20160726232508im_/http://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/modules/features/wiz_bean_content_deck_list/icons/decklist_download.png)
